# seller-requested-cancellation >> seller-requested-cancellation (OpenBookingApprovalFlow >> Multiple)

**Booking Flow:** OpenBookingApprovalFlow

**Opportunity Type:** Multiple

**Feature:** Cancellation / Seller Requested Cancellation (Implemented) 

**Test:**  Seller cancellation of order request.

A successful cancellation of order by seller, Order in feed should have status SellerCancelled

### Running only this test

```bash
npm start -- --runInBand test/features/cancellation/seller-requested-cancellation/implemented/seller-requested-cancellation-test.js
```
